msg:Very good. The high-end atmosphere is clean and tidy. The service is considerate. The European-style architecture is very comfortable. It is said that it was the place where Mr. Zhang Jian, the number one scholar in the Qing Dynasty, received literati. After many expansions, it became the century-old store it is now. The location is super good. I have spent a lot of time here. Less than 15 meters from the road is the 5A-level Haohe Scenic Area. There is a cruise ship dock. It is convenient to take a walk by the Haohe River after breakfast and dinner. For dinner, friends arranged to have dinner in a window box and enjoy the scenery, either in the room or in the corridor. Seeing the clear water of the Hao River, if you get up early, you can also see a few dragon boat enthusiasts rowing dragon boats, which is pleasing to the eye. Although it is in a bustling downtown area, you can't hear the noise of the city at all in the room. Watch it in the room at night The lights in the Haohe Scenic Area are also very beautiful. It is only about 100 meters away from the most prosperous South Street in Nantong. If you are coming to Nantong for travel, business and vacation, Youfei is still the first choice.
